Topics
This chapter discusses:
                                                                This section explains what is a sale or trade. It also ex-
                                                                plains certain transactions and events that are treated as
 • What Is a Sale or Trade,                                     sales or trades.
 • Basis of Investment Property,
                                                                  A sale is generally a transfer of property for money or a
 • Adjusted Basis,                                              mortgage, note, or other promise to pay money.
 • How To Figure Gain or Loss,                                    A trade is a transfer of property for other property or
 • Nontaxable Trades,                                           services, and may be taxed in the same way as a sale.
 • Transfers Between Spouses,                                   Sale or trade of digital assets. For U.S. tax purposes,
 • Related Party Transactions,                                  digital assets are considered property, not currency. A dig-
                                                                ital asset is stored electronically and it can be bought,
 • Capital Gains and Losses,                                    sold, owned, transferred, or traded. If a particular asset
 • Reporting Capital Gains and Losses, and                      has the characteristics of a digital asset, it will be treated
                                                                as a digital asset for federal income tax purposes.
 • Special Rules for Traders in Securities or
    Commodities.                                                   Digital assets are any digital representations of value
                                                                that are recorded on a cryptographically secured distrib-
                                                                uted ledger or any similar technology. For example, digital
